! Title: AdBlock DNS Lite
! Description: 适用于 AdGuard、AdGuardHome 的去广告合并规则，每 8 个小时更新一次。规则源：AdGuard Base filter、AdGuard Chinese filter、AdGuard Mobile Ads filter、AdGuard DNS filter、AdRules DNS List、CJX's Annoyance List、EasyList、EasyList China、EasyPrivacy、xinggsf mv、xinggsf rule、jiekouAD、1Hosts (Lite)、AWAvenue Ads Rule、DNS-Blocklists Light、Hblock、OISD Basic、StevenBlack hosts、Pollock hosts、anti-AD、AdRules、Phishing URL Blocklist、Online Malicious URL Blocklist、PeterLowe、OISD Big、DanPollock、SmartTV、HageziUltimate、1Host (Xtra)。Lite 版仅针对国内域名拦截。
